 <div class="qodef-content-inner">
    <div class="qodef-title qodef-standard-type qodef-content-left-alignment qodef-animation-no" style="height:250px;" data-height="250">
        <div class="qodef-title-image"></div>
        <div class="qodef-title-holder" style="height:250px;">
            <div class="qodef-container clearfix">
                <div class="qodef-container-inner">
                    <div class="qodef-title-subtitle-holder" style="">
                        <div class="qodef-title-subtitle-holder-inner">
                                                        <h1><span>Tutorial Hadoop multi node installation</span></h1>
                                                                                                                    </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

	<div class="qodef-container">
				<div class="qodef-container-inner">
				<div class="qodef-two-columns-66-33 qodef-content-has-sidebar  clearfix">
		<div class="qodef-column1 qodef-content-left-from-sidebar">
			<div class="qodef-column-inner">
				<div class="qodef-blog-holder qodef-blog-single">
					<article id="post-5119" class="post-5119 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-hadoop-labs tag-apache-hadoop-en tag-hadoop-cluster-en tag-hadoop-multi-node-installation-en tag-map-reduce-en">
	<div class="qodef-post-content">
			<div class="qodef-post-image">
			<img width="300" height="293" src="./Tutorial Hadoop multi node installation - intellitech.pro_files/hadoop-300x293.png" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="hadoop logo">	</div>
		<div class="qodef-post-text">
			<div class="qodef-post-text-inner">
				<div class="qodef-blog-standard-post-date">
	<span class="date">05</span>
	<span class="month">Dec</span>
</div>				<div class="qodef-blog-standard-info-holder">
					<h2 class="qodef-post-title">
	Tutorial Hadoop multi node installation</h2>					<div class="qodef-post-info">
						<div class="qodef-post-info-author">by <a class="qodef-post-info-author-link" href="https://intellitech.pro/author/nizar/">Nizar Ellouze</a></div>
<div class="qodef-post-info-category">
    in <a href="https://intellitech.pro/category/hadoop-labs/" rel="category tag">Hadoop labs</a></div><div class="qodef-post-info-comments-holder"><a class="qodef-post-info-comments" href="https://intellitech.pro/tutorial-hadoop-multi-node-installation/#comments" target="_self">Comments</a></div>					</div>
				</div>
				<p>In this tutorial we will see how to install a Hadoop multi node nodes by doing the following steps:</p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><b>step1:</b> You need to ensure that hadoop is installed (single node mode) on all pcs (masters+ slaves). If not use this <a href="http://intellitech.pro/hadoop-first-lab/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">link</a> to do it </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><b>step 2:</b> Now let’s configure the pcs to work on multinode cluster, as an example we will use two slaves and one master:</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Add all host names to&nbsp;/etc/hosts directory in all Machines (Master and Slave nodes):</span></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta -->

		<div id="crayon-639c06c1e725f003461011" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-shell-default crayon-font-ubuntu-mono crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style="margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; height: auto;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="tab-size: 4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; z-index: 0; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;">    sudo gedit /etc/hosts</textarea></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="position: relative; z-index: 1; overflow: hidden;">
				<table class="crayon-table" style="">
					<tbody><tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-639c06c1e725f003461011-1">1</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-639c06c1e725f003461011-1"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">sudo </span><span class="crayon-v">gedit</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">/</span><span class="crayon-v">etc</span><span class="crayon-o">/</span><span class="crayon-v">hosts</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</tbody></table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0014 seconds] -->
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"># Add following hostname and their ip in host table</span><br>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Suppose that your slaves address are : 192.168.0.151 and 192.168.0.152. And the master address is: 192.168.0.150</span></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta -->

		<div id="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-shell-default crayon-font-ubuntu-mono crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style="margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; height: auto;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="tab-size: 4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; z-index: 0; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;">    192.168.0.150 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HadoopMaster
    192.168.0.151 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HadoopSlave1
    192.168.0.152 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HadoopSlave2</textarea></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="position: relative; z-index: 1; overflow: hidden;">
				<table class="crayon-table" style="">
					<tbody><tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302-2">2</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302-3">3</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302-1"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-cn">192.168.0.150</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="crayon-i">HadoopMaster</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302-2"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-cn">192.168.0.151</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="crayon-i">HadoopSlave1</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-639c06c1e726b538382302-3"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-cn">192.168.0.152</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="crayon-v">HadoopSlave2</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</tbody></table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0002 seconds] -->
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">login with hduser, then install rsync and reboot the pc</span></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta -->

		<div id="crayon-639c06c1e726e459529333" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-shell-default crayon-font-ubuntu-mono crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style="margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; height: auto;">

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">SSH Configuration:</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><b>On the master node</b> fire the following command for sharing public SSH key ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub&nbsp;file (of HadoopMaster node) to authorized_keys file of hduser@HadoopSlave1 and also on hduser@HadoopSlave1 (in&nbsp;$HOME/.ssh/authorized_keys)</span></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta -->

		<div id="crayon-639c06c1e72a6099212177" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-shell-default crayon-font-ubuntu-mono crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style="margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; height: auto;">

    ssh-copy-id -i $HOME/.ssh/id_rsa.pub hduser@HadoopSlave1

				</tbody></table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0001 seconds] -->

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">execute word count example:</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">in the masternode (always, clients should only talk to masternode ):</span></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta -->

		<div id="crayon-639c06c1e72c4562514637" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-shell-default crayon-font-ubuntu-mono crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style="margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; height: auto;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="tab-size: 4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; z-index: 0; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;">    hdfs dfs -mkdir /test/
    hdfs dfs -copyFromLocal wordCountinput.txt /test/
    hadoop jar /usr/local/hadoop/share/hadoop/mapreduce/hadoop-mapreduce-examples-2.6.0.jar wordcount /test/wordCountinput.txt /test/output/</textarea></div>
